\index{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Latin1@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Latin1}!physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Latin1()}{PHYSFS\_utf8FromLatin1()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{png_8h_ac9c84fa68bbad002983e35ce3663c686}{void} P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Latin1 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const} char $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a632ba02500231e5f6f6df2e4cb71c818}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64}}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a U\+T\+F-\/8 string to a Latin1 string. 

Latin1 strings are 8-\/bits per character\+: a popular \char`\"{}high A\+S\+C\+I\+I\char`\"{} encoding.

To ensure that the destination buffer is large enough for the conversion, please allocate a buffer that is double the size of the source buffer. U\+T\+F-\/8 expands latin1 codepoints over 127 from 1 to 2 bytes, so the string may grow in some cases.

Strings that don\textquotesingle{}t fit in the destination buffer will be truncated, but will always be null-\/terminated and never have an incomplete U\+T\+F-\/8 sequence at the end. If the buffer length is 0, this function does nothing.

Please note that we do not supply a U\+T\+F-\/8 to Latin1 converter, since Latin1 can\textquotesingle{}t express most Unicode codepoints. It\textquotesingle{}s a legacy encoding; you should be converting away from it at all times.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & Null-\/terminated source string in Latin1 format. \\
\hline
{\em dst} & Buffer to store converted U\+T\+F-\/8 string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & Size, in bytes, of destination buffer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{physfs_8h_ac4fdac7e09fb03ccdccdeed997f09c1a}\label{physfs_8h_ac4fdac7e09fb03ccdccdeed997f09c1a}} 
\index{physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}!P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2}}
\index{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2}!physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2()}{PHYSFS\_utf8FromUcs2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{png_8h_ac9c84fa68bbad002983e35ce3663c686}{void} P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const} \hyperlink{physfs_8h_ac4d1c74e276b04ef993530a405553574}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint16} $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a632ba02500231e5f6f6df2e4cb71c818}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64}}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a U\+C\+S-\/2 string to a U\+T\+F-\/8 string. 

U\+C\+S-\/2 strings are 16-\/bits per character\+: {\ttfamily T\+C\+H\+AR} on Windows, when building with Unicode support.

To ensure that the destination buffer is large enough for the conversion, please allocate a buffer that is double the size of the source buffer. U\+T\+F-\/8 never uses more than 32-\/bits per character, so while it may shrink a U\+C\+S-\/2 string, it may also expand it.

Strings that don\textquotesingle{}t fit in the destination buffer will be truncated, but will always be null-\/terminated and never have an incomplete U\+T\+F-\/8 sequence at the end. If the buffer length is 0, this function does nothing.

Please note that U\+C\+S-\/2 is not U\+T\+F-\/16; we do not support the \char`\"{}surrogate\char`\"{} values at this time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & Null-\/terminated source string in U\+C\+S-\/2 format. \\
\hline
{\em dst} & Buffer to store converted U\+T\+F-\/8 string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & Size, in bytes, of destination buffer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{physfs_8h_ac18c9c45db1be6fd26be19d0f4d25a60}\label{physfs_8h_ac18c9c45db1be6fd26be19d0f4d25a60}} 
\index{physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}!P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4}}
\index{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4}!physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4()}{PHYSFS\_utf8FromUcs4()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{png_8h_ac9c84fa68bbad002983e35ce3663c686}{void} P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+From\+Ucs4 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const} \hyperlink{physfs_8h_aae011b45ebd619edb193fe196e1f5f74}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint32} $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a632ba02500231e5f6f6df2e4cb71c818}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64}}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a U\+C\+S-\/4 string to a U\+T\+F-\/8 string. 

U\+C\+S-\/4 strings are 32-\/bits per character\+: {\ttfamily wchar\+\_\+t} on Unix.

To ensure that the destination buffer is large enough for the conversion, please allocate a buffer that is the same size as the source buffer. U\+T\+F-\/8 never uses more than 32-\/bits per character, so while it may shrink a U\+C\+S-\/4 string, it will never expand it.

Strings that don\textquotesingle{}t fit in the destination buffer will be truncated, but will always be null-\/terminated and never have an incomplete U\+T\+F-\/8 sequence at the end. If the buffer length is 0, this function does nothing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & Null-\/terminated source string in U\+C\+S-\/4 format. \\
\hline
{\em dst} & Buffer to store converted U\+T\+F-\/8 string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & Size, in bytes, of destination buffer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{physfs_8h_a0ab51c265f7ca4e8218d6c74b4f43401}\label{physfs_8h_a0ab51c265f7ca4e8218d6c74b4f43401}} 
\index{physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}!P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2}}
\index{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2}!physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2()}{PHYSFS\_utf8ToUcs2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const} char $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_ac4d1c74e276b04ef993530a405553574}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint16} $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a632ba02500231e5f6f6df2e4cb71c818}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64}}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a U\+T\+F-\/8 string to a U\+C\+S-\/2 string. 

U\+C\+S-\/2 strings are 16-\/bits per character\+: {\ttfamily T\+C\+H\+AR} on Windows, when building with Unicode support.

To ensure that the destination buffer is large enough for the conversion, please allocate a buffer that is double the size of the source buffer. U\+T\+F-\/8 uses from one to four bytes per character, but U\+C\+S-\/2 always uses two, so an entirely low-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II string will double in size!

Strings that don\textquotesingle{}t fit in the destination buffer will be truncated, but will always be null-\/terminated and never have an incomplete U\+C\+S-\/2 sequence at the end. If the buffer length is 0, this function does nothing.

Please note that U\+C\+S-\/2 is not U\+T\+F-\/16; we do not support the \char`\"{}surrogate\char`\"{} values at this time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & Null-\/terminated source string in U\+T\+F-\/8 format. \\
\hline
{\em dst} & Buffer to store converted U\+C\+S-\/2 string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & Size, in bytes, of destination buffer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{physfs_8h_a3ff1045e71cd4c14607973da7bfc41e5}\label{physfs_8h_a3ff1045e71cd4c14607973da7bfc41e5}} 
\index{physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}!P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4}}
\index{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4@{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4}!physfs.\+h@{physfs.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4()}{PHYSFS\_utf8ToUcs4()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{png_8h_ac9c84fa68bbad002983e35ce3663c686}{void} P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+utf8\+To\+Ucs4 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const} char $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_aae011b45ebd619edb193fe196e1f5f74}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint32} $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a632ba02500231e5f6f6df2e4cb71c818}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64}}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a U\+T\+F-\/8 string to a U\+C\+S-\/4 string. 

U\+C\+S-\/4 strings are 32-\/bits per character\+: {\ttfamily wchar\+\_\+t} on Unix.

To ensure that the destination buffer is large enough for the conversion, please allocate a buffer that is four times the size of the source buffer. U\+T\+F-\/8 uses from one to four bytes per character, but U\+C\+S-\/4 always uses four, so an entirely low-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II string will quadruple in size!

Strings that don\textquotesingle{}t fit in the destination buffer will be truncated, but will always be null-\/terminated and never have an incomplete U\+C\+S-\/4 sequence at the end. If the buffer length is 0, this function does nothing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & Null-\/terminated source string in U\+T\+F-\/8 format. \\
\hline
{\em dst} & Buffer to store converted U\+C\+S-\/4 string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & Size, in bytes, of destination buffer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+write\+S\+L\+E64 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{struct_p_h_y_s_f_s___file}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+\+File} $\ast$}]{file,  }\item[{\hyperlink{physfs_8h_a88c5f1d7b088888c729b22644651c9f5}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+sint64}}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert and write a signed 64-\/bit littleendian value. 

Convenience function. Convert a signed 64-\/bit value from the platform\textquotesingle{}s native byte order to littleendian and write it to a file.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file} & Physics\+FS file handle to which to write. \\
\hline
{\em val} & Value to convert and write. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
zero on failure, non-\/zero on success. On failure, you can find out what went wrong from \hyperlink{physfs_8h_a9f78e4ab560885fd10202988d2fff1b6}{P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+get\+Last\+Error()}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Remember, P\+H\+Y\+S\+F\+S\+\_\+uint64 is only 32 bits on platforms without any sort of 64-\/bit support. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
